The takeaway I ordered after checking in arrived at the hotel around 10 o'clock. The takeaway guy couldn't get into the passenger elevator. I understood that at that time, I had taken a shower and changed into pajamas. I wanted to contact the front desk to see if the robot or manual delivery was sent up, and told me to come down to pick it up myself. After many negotiations, it was not possible. Then I could only change clothes and go down to pick it up. This experience was also quite speechless. I slept until almost three o'clock at night, and woke up. I was awakened by the sound of water on the top of the bathroom. I think my sleep is not that shallow. The sound continued until about five o'clock. There may be more later, but I was too sleepy to fall asleep at that time. I got up at eight o'clock in the morning to pack my things, and accidentally found that there were things behind the bedside table that were not mine. It felt like underwear. With this hygiene situation, I think I have to question whether towels and cups can be replaced and disinfected for each guest! The last breakfast was not as good as the breakfast I had at Hanting ten years ago. There was basically no hot food before 8:30. The dining area was large but there was not much food on offer. I had no appetite at all. In the end, I had some fried rice, two small pieces of crispy meat, and a cup of yogurt. Not to mention how high the starch content of the crispy meat was, I couldn't accept it when I put it in my mouth and found that it was cold! ! When I left the restaurant, I reminded the handsome guy who collected the meal coupons that the dish was cold, but he didn't seem to react. There were also front desk staff who took the food like the guests, sat in the restaurant to eat, and then went to work at the front desk (when I went to the front desk to ask about the parking coupons, I found that I met them in the restaurant).
How to say it? It's outrageous, quite outrageous, outrageous to the point of outrageous! The management team of this hotel has a long way to go, so take care of yourself.

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in June 2021
info:Family
info:67 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted August 16, 2021
msg:   端午節帶着寶寶全家去無錫玩兒，入住了這家酒店感覺良好。酒店距離無錫火車站很近，如行李不多走走都行。酒店開了很多年了，但近期徹底重裝後名字都改了。酒店大堂裝修的相當氣派而且品味不俗。入住期間這家酒店的大堂副理給人印象深刻，大多數酒店這個職位的工作人員往往坐在一張大桌子邊上，或者那張桌子邊上壓根沒人，你不問什麼一般也不會主動搭理你。而這家酒店的大堂副理工作卻非常主動，給人充滿活力的感覺，這位美女大約三四十歲，穿着制服顯得十分幹練，似乎總能捕捉到客人潛在的需求。我多次經過大堂她都是這樣一種狀態，很是難得。酒店客房也是全新裝修，設施良好。我們入住的那間客房可清晰看到進出車站的火車，寶寶是火車迷高興壞了。酒店早餐也品質良好，最讓人意外的是吃早餐的餐廳晚上是精品火鍋，味道、服務、價格均令人滿意，以至於第2天晚上又去吃了，連服務員都好奇問我們是否是住在附近的居民。總之這家酒店地理位置優越，儘管靠近火車站，但並不嘈雜，硬件及軟件均十分不錯，值得推薦。
----------------------------------------
